12/03/2022, 12:16â€¯pm - +91 93198 39861: Do we have any course or videos related to deep learning model optimization?

12/03/2022, 12:58â€¯pm - +91 6386 461 149: Three type of optimization you can prefer

1. Knowledge Distillation: Student-Teacher Learning making use of KL Divergence to compare two models.

Majorly models like Transformer goes through this process as they are having a lot of parameters that why you can see, distillery, DistillRoberta in Hugging face.

2. Model Quantization: FP16, FP32, FP64 previously we have apex module by nvidia but now you can easily find this implementation in pytorch trainer

3. Model Pruning: Removing the weighted connection in model, to reduce its size majorly prefers for edge devices.
12/03/2022, 1:00â€¯pm - +91 6386 461 149: The above are major one which are generally preferred depending upon the use case and size of the model, and the disadvantage is you will see a reduction in predection, your model might not be that good after size reduction and optimization but inference time will reduce.

26/03/2022, 7:41â€¯am - +91 98745 88202: I recently took the test, and this is what one of the current employee advised:

The test will most probably contain 6-7 MCQs on Stat and DS fundamentals like Hypothesis testing and all.
2 Python competitive coding questions of 10-12 lines of problem statement, sample input, sample output and 10-15 hidden testcases.

You should try getting all the MCQs right at any cost and then pass at least few hidden testcases of atleast one code, if not all.
Passing 4-5 testcases of 1 of the codes and correct MCQs will be sufficient to qualify most of the times.
Coding questions are really difficult sometimes.

All the best!

26/03/2022, 1:06â€¯pm - +91 80958 17985: Tiger Analytics:

1st round:
 
Online test on:
Python coding
SQL coding

2nd round:

1.	You have 30records with 10 features. You made 10 trees(n_estimators).Data is divided into 80/20 ratio(train/test set). After one epoch, Training accuracy you got 80% but test 	accuracy you got 60 %. Now what would you do to handle this.
2.	In share trading, a buyer buys shares and sells on a future date. Given the stock price of n days, the trader is allowed to make at most k transactions, where a new transaction can only start after the previous transaction is complete, find out the maximum profit that a share trader could have made.
3.	you have 25 cards of 5 different colour. what is the probability if picking 2 different color cards.
4.	Probability of - atleast 1 plane goes away every 5 min  = 15%. What is the probability of atleast 1 plane go every 30 minute?
5.	What is the probability that a point will lie close to circumference of the circle than to center.
6.	There is one categorical feature which is having 3 catergories.How do you deal with this?(then folow up question when I told about dummies) How do you get the dummies? How the metrics gets affected.

3rd round(DS final round):

1.	Find the largest cumulative sum from a list having -ve and +integers.
2.	How to draw AUC graph?

16/09/2022, 8:53â€¯pm - +91 99130 07097: Hi All,

Can  someone please explain p value to explain in interview?

I read it many times but not able to explain to interviewer
17/09/2022, 1:38â€¯am - +91 76760 31474: P-value is the probability value that the null hypothesis is true (if p > 0.05).

If the p-value is low (p < 0.05) then the alternative hypothesis is true.

High p-values indicate that our evidence is not strong enough to suggest an effect exists, so null hypothesis.

Example: 
For P < 0.05

It means that column/dataframe is less significant/importance and we will reject the Null Hypothesis and accept the Alternative Hypothesis.
17/09/2022, 1:43â€¯am - +91 76760 31474: For more details, go through Null & Alternative Hypothesis.

Also, understand the central limit theorem and confidence level (for 5% (0.05) except 95%)

23/02/2023, 9:02â€¯pm - +91 96969 00002: Enough of #pytorch , so what to do? Welcome to session on pytorch lightening, register  ğŸ‘‰  https://lnkd.in/gVHmTxiz #share

PyTorch Lightning is a powerful and easy-to-use framework for deep learning that streamlines the training process, making it more efficient and less error-prone. With PyTorch Lightning, you can focus on defining and designing your neural network models, while the framework takes care of the underlying training code. It also provides a range of advanced features such as distributed training, GPU acceleration, and automatic logging, which can help you optimize your training process and scale up your deep learning projects. By learning PyTorch Lightning, you can improve your productivity and efficiency in deep learning development and research, making it a valuable skill for anyone interested in this field.

14/08/2023, 5:14â€¯pm - +91 90803 38368: *DPO paper implementation for making model respond in a way you want to:*
Hi everyone. I recently posted a video on the explanation of the Direct Preference Optimization paper where I had some great responses for it by becoming the first recommendation by google search engine when you search for dpo paper explanation. That was part 1 where the paper was discussed in detail with the comparison with rlhf which it can replace but in a computationally efficient manner.

In this second part of DPO, I have implemented the algorithm to train a model as per my preference. To check if it really aligns the preferences a coding model was taken and was made to generate chat and it provided some impressive results. This if scaled to a great extent it can potentially be one of the top methods to make your model generate responses by your preferences. For this I have used TRL library from HuggingFace to train a model by using DPO. 

If interested to make your model respond in a way you want it to respond check out the following detailed implementation of finetuning and preference optimization of model using DPO in the following video link. Code is provided in the github repo for which the link is available in the description of the video
Video Link: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=P1ji_HlNQ-s
